CAPTR î—STʀT IN LîF


î wuz bᴙn in Ŧ yr 1632, in Ŧ sity o York, o a gød famly,
Ŧō n o Ŧt kuntry, m foŦr byiñ a fᴙenr o Bremen, ø
setld frst at Hul.  Y got a gød estāt bî mrcandîs, & lyviñ
of hiz trād, livd aftrwrdz at York, x Ψens y had mᴚyd m
muŦr, høz rylā§nz wr nāmd Robinson, a v gød famly in Ŧt
kuntry, & x høm î wuz kold Robinson Kreutznaer; bt, bî Ŧ
yøzøᴥl corruption o wrdz in Eñglnd, wy ʀ nŭ kold—nā wy kol
ŭrselvz & rît ŭr nām—Crusoe; & sō m kmpanynz alwāz kold
my.

î had 2 eldr bruŦrz, 1 o høm wuz lieutenant-colonel t an
Iñgli§ rejimnt o føt in Flanders, fᴙmrly kmandd bî Ŧ fāmus
Krnl Lockhart, & wuz kild at Ŧ batl nyr Dunkirk agānst Ŧ
Spanyʀdz.  Ψut bykām o m sekond bruŦr î nevr nø, eny mᴙ Ŧan
m foŦr ᴙ muŦr nø Ψut bykām o my.

Byiñ Ŧ Ŧrd sun o Ŧ famly & n bred t eny trād, m hed
bygan t b fild v rly w rambliñ Ŧots.  M foŦr, ø wuz
v ān§ent, had givn my a kompᴥtnt §ᴚ o lrniñ, az fʀ az
house-education & a kuntry fry skøl jenruly gō, & dyzînd my
f Ŧ lo; bt î wød b satisfîd w nuŦiñ bt gōiñ t sy; &
m inklinā§n t Ŧis led my sō stroñly agānst Ŧ wil, nā, Ŧ
kmandz o m foŦr, & agānst ol Ŧ entrytyz & prswā§nz o
m muŦr & uŦr frendz, Ŧt Ŧᴚ symd t b sumŦiñ fātl in
Ŧt prōpensity o nācr, tendiñ dîrektly t Ŧ lîf o mizry Ψic
wuz t byfol my.

M foŦr, a wîz & grāv man, gāv my syryus & xelent kŭnsl
agānst Ψut y fᴙso wuz m dyzîn.  Y kold my 1 mᴙniñ intø hiz
cāmbr, Ψᴚ y wuz knfînd bî Ŧ gŭt, & expostulated v wʀmly
w my upon Ŧis subjekt.  Y askd my Ψut ryznz, mᴙ Ŧan a myr
wondriñ inklinā§n, î had f lyviñ foŦr’s hŭs & m nātiv
kuntry, Ψᴚ î mît b wel intrōdøsd, & had a prospect o rāziñ
m fᴙcn bî aplikā§n & industry, w a lîf o yz & ple§r.

supyryr fᴙcunz on Ŧ uŦr, ø went abrod upon advencrz, t rîz

tø fʀ bylō my; Ŧt mîn wuz Ŧ midl stāt, ᴙ Ψut mît b kold
Ŧ upr stā§n o lō lîf, Ψic y had fŭnd, bî loñ xpyryens,
wuz Ŧ best stāt in Ŧ wrld, Ŧ mōst søtd t hømn hapynes, n
xpōzd t Ŧ mizryz & hʀd§ips, Ŧ labour & sufriñz o Ŧ

ambi§n, & envy o Ŧ upr pʀt o mankînd.  Y tōld my î mît
juj o Ŧ hapynes o Ŧis stāt bî Ŧis 1 ñ—viz. Ŧt Ŧis wuz
Ŧ stāt o lîf Ψic ol uŦr p envyd; Ŧt kiñz h
fryqently lamentd Ŧ mizrᴥbl konsᴥqens o byiñ bᴙn t grāt

testimōny t Ŧis, az Ŧ standrd o felicity, Ψen y prād t h

wød n sys t prā f my, yet y wød vencr t s t my, Ŧt
if î did tāk Ŧis føli§ step, God wød n bles my, & î §ød
h ly§r hyraftr t ryflekt upon haviñ neglektd hiz kŭnsl Ψen
Ŧᴚ mît b nun t asist in m rykuvry.

î obzrvd in Ŧis last pʀt o hiz diskᴙs, Ψic wuz trøly profetik,
Ŧō î supōz m foŦr did n nō it t b sō himself—î s, î

spōk o m bruŦr ø wuz kild: & Ŧt Ψen y spōk o m haviñ
ly§r t rypent, & nun t asist my, y wuz sō møvd Ŧt y brōk

î wuz sinsyrly afektd w Ŧis diskᴙs, &, indyd, ø kød b
uŦrwîz? & î ryzolvd n t ᴥ o gōiñ abrod eny mᴙ, bt t

ātyn yrs ōld, Ψic wuz tø lāt t gō aprentis t a trād ᴙ

Ŧis pøt m muŦr intø a grāt pa§n; § tōld my § nø it wød b

xpre§nz az § nø m foŦr had yøzd t my; & Ŧt, in §ᴙt, if

§ød nevr h Ŧᴚ knsent t it; Ŧt f r pʀt § wød n

CAPTR II—SLāVRY & ESKāP


Ŧt yvil infløens Ψic kᴚyd my frst awā x m foŦr’s

    “F sudn j¤z, lîk griefs, konfŭnd at frst.”

CAPTR IV—FRST WYX ON Ŧ îLND


Ψen î wākt it wuz brod dā, Ŧ weŦr klyr, & Ŧ stᴙm abātd,

M nxt kᴚ wuz f sum amøni§n & ʀmz.  Ŧᴚ wr 2 v gød

î had 3 encouragements—1st, a smøŦ, kom sy; 2ndly, Ŧ tîd

Az î imajind, sō it wuz.  Ŧᴚ apyrd byfᴙ my a litl ōpeniñ o

Bt hyr î had lîk t h sufrd a sekond §iprek, Ψic, if î had,

drîviñ up hîr, î at leñŦ fŭnd mîself in Ŧ mŭŦ o a litl

yŦr sîd w m ax, til î brot it t b Ŧin az a plank, &
Ŧen dub it smøŦ w m adze.  It z trø, bî Ŧis meŦᴥd î kød ā
bt 1 bᴙd ŭt o a hōl try; bt Ŧis î had nō remᴥdy f bt
pā§ns, eny mᴙ Ŧan î had f Ŧ prōdijus dyl o tîm & labour
Ψic it tøk my up t ā a plank ᴙ bᴙd: bt m tîm ᴙ labour wuz
litl wrŦ, & sō it wuz az wel empl¤d 1 wā az anuŦr.

Hŭevr, î mād my a tābl & a cᴚ, az î obzrvd abuv, in Ŧ frst
plās; & Ŧis î did ŭt o Ŧ §ᴙt pysez o bᴙdz Ŧt î brot on
m raft x Ŧ §ip.  Bt Ψen î had rot ŭt sum bᴙdz az abuv,
î mād lʀj §elvz, o Ŧ bredŦ o a føt & a haf, 1 ovr
anuŦr ol aloñ 1 sîd o m kāv, t lā ol m tølz, nālz &
ironwork on; &, in a wrd, t seprᴥt evryŦiñ at lʀj intø Ŧᴚ
plāsez, Ŧt î mît kum yzily at Ŧem.  î knocked pysez intø Ŧ wol
o Ŧ rok t hañ m gunz & ol Ŧiñs Ŧt wød hañ up; sō Ŧt,
had m kāv byn t b syn, it løkt lîk a jenrl magaz o ol
nesesᴚy Ŧiñs; & had evryŦiñ sō redy at m hand, Ŧt it wuz a
grāt ple§r t my t sy ol m gødz in suc ᴙdr, & espe§ly t
fînd m stok o ol necessaries sō grāt.

& nŭ it wuz Ŧt î bygan t kyp a jrnl o evry dā’s empl¤mnt;
f, indyd, at frst î wuz in tø muc hry, & n ōnly hry az t
labour, bt in tø muc discomposure o mînd; & m jrnl wød h
byn føl o meny dul Ŧiñs; f xampl, î must h sed Ŧus:
“30_th_.—Aftr î had got t §ᴙ, & eskāpt drŭniñ, insted o byiñ
Ŧankføl t God f m dylivrans, haviñ frst vomitd, w Ŧ grāt
qontity o solt wotr Ψic had got intø m stumik, & rykuvriñ
mîself a litl, î ran ŭ Ŧ §ᴙ riñiñ m handz & bytiñ m
hed & fās, xklāmiñ at m mizry, & krîiñ ŭt, ‘î wuz undun,
undun!’ til, tîrd & fānt, î wuz forst t lî dŭn on Ŧ grŭnd t
rypōz, bt durst n slyp f fyr o byiñ dyvŭrd.”

Sum dāz aftr Ŧis, & aftr î had byn on bᴙd Ŧ §ip, & got ol
Ŧt î kød ŭt o r, yet î kød n forbear getiñ up t Ŧ top o
a litl mŭntn & løkiñ ŭt t sy, in hōps o syiñ a §ip; Ŧen
fansy at a vast distns î spîd a sāl, plyz mîself w Ŧ hōps o
it, & Ŧen aftr løkiñ stedily, til î wuz olmōst blînd, løz it
qît, & sit dŭn & wyp lîk a cîld, & Ŧus inkrys m mizry bî
m foly.

Bt haviñ gotn ovr Ŧyz Ŧiñs in sum me§r, & haviñ setld
m hŭshōld staf & habitā§n, mād my a tābl & a cᴚ, & ol
az hansm ŭ my az î kød, î bygan t kyp m jrnl; o Ψic î
§al hyr giv u Ŧ kopy (Ŧō in it wil b tōld ol Ŧyz
pʀtikølrz ovr agān) az loñ az it lastd; f haviñ nō mᴙ iñk, î
wuz forst t lyv it of.




CAPTR V—BILDZ A HŭS—Ŧ JRNL


Septembr 30, 1659.—î, pør mizrᴥbl Robinson Crusoe, byiñ §iprekt
døriñ a dredføl stᴙm in Ŧ ofiñ, kām on §ᴙ on Ŧis dizml,
unfᴙcønᴥt îlnd, Ψic î kold “Ŧ îlnd o Despᴚ”; ol Ŧ rest
o Ŧ §ip’s kumpany byiñ drŭnd, & mîself olmōst ded.

Ol Ŧ rest o Ŧ dā î spent in afliktiñ mîself at Ŧ dizml
srkumstansz î wuz brot t—viz. î had nyŦr fød, hŭs, klōz,
wepn, nᴙ plās t flî t; & in despᴚ o eny rylyf, so nuŦiñ

mrdrd bî savājz, ᴙ stʀvd t deŦ f wont o fød.  At Ŧ

_Oktōbr_ 1.—In Ŧ mᴙniñ î so, t m grāt srpîz, Ŧ §ip had
flōtd w Ŧ hî tîd, & wuz drivn on §ᴙ agān muc nyrr Ŧ
îlnd; Ψic, az it wuz sum kumfrt, on 1 hand—f, syiñ r set

g on bᴙd, & g sum fød & necessaries ŭt o r f m
rylyf—sō, on Ŧ uŦr hand, it rynød m gryf at Ŧ los o m
komradz, ø, î imajind, if wy had ol stād on bᴙd, mît h
sāvd Ŧ §ip, ᴙ, at lyst, Ŧt Ŧā wød n h byn ol drŭnd
az Ŧā wr; & Ŧt, had Ŧ men byn sāvd, wy mît prhaps h
bilt us a bōt ŭt o Ŧ røinz o Ŧ §ip t h kᴚyd us t sum
uŦr pʀt o Ŧ wrld.  î spent grāt pʀt o Ŧis dā in prplexiñ

it kontinød rāniñ, Ŧō w nō wind at ol.

_X Ŧ 1st o Oktōbr t Ŧ 24th_.—Ol Ŧyz dāz entîrly spent in

Ŧō w sum intrvlz o fᴚ weŦr; bt it symz Ŧis wuz Ŧ

_Oct._ 20.—î overset m raft, & ol Ŧ gødz î had got upon it; bt,

_Oct._ 25.—It rānd ol nît & ol dā, w sum gusts o wind;

_Oct._ 26.—î wokt ŭ Ŧ §ᴙ olmōst ol dā, t fînd ŭt a plās

_Nov._ 14, 15, 16.—Ŧyz 3 dāz î spent in mākiñ litl sqᴚ

_Nov._ 17.—Ŧis dā î bygan t dig byhînd m tent intø Ŧ rok, t ā

_Nōt_.—3 Ŧiñs î wontd xsydiñly f Ŧis wrk—viz. a pickaxe, a

_Dec._ 24.—Muc rān ol nît & ol dā.  Nō strriñ ŭt.

_Dec._ 26.—Nō rān, & Ŧ rŦ muc kølr Ŧan byfᴙ, &

_Dec._ 27.—Kild a yuñ gōt, & lamed anuŦr, sō Ŧt î kot it

_Janøᴚy_ 1.—V hot stil: bt î went abrod rly & lāt w m

Ψen Ŧis wol wuz fini§t, & Ŧ ŭtsîd dubl fenst, w a trf

Døriñ Ŧis tîm î mād m rŭndz in Ŧ wødz f gām evry dā Ψen

manajiñ m hŭshōld afᴚz, î fŭnd mîself wontiñ in meny Ŧiñs,

CAPTR VI—IL & CONSCIENCE-STRICKEN


Ψen î kām dŭn t Ŧ §ip î fŭnd it strānjly rymøvd.  Ŧ
forecastle, Ψic lā byfᴙ bᴚyd in sand, wuz hyvd up at lyst six
fyt, & Ŧ strn, Ψic wuz brōk in pysez & pʀtd x Ŧ rest

Ŧt sîd nxt r strn, Ŧt Ψᴚaz Ŧᴚ wuz a grāt plās o wotr
byfᴙ, sō Ŧt î kød n kum wiŦin a qᴙtr o a mîl o Ŧ rek
wiŦŭt swimiñ î kød nŭ wok qît up t r Ψen Ŧ tîd wuz ŭt.
î wuz srprîzd w Ŧis at frst, bt søn knklødd it must b dun bî
Ŧ rŦqāk; & az bî Ŧis vîōlens Ŧ §ip wuz mᴙ brōk ōpen Ŧan
fᴙmrly, sō meny Ŧiñs kām dāly on §ᴙ, Ψic Ŧ sy had løsnd,
& Ψic Ŧ winds & wotr rōld bî dᴥgryz t Ŧ land.

Ŧis hōly dîvrtd m Ŧots x Ŧ dyzîn o rymøviñ m
habitā§n, & î bizyd mîself mîtily, Ŧt dā espe§ly, in
srciñ ΨeŦr î kød ā eny wā intø Ŧ §ip; bt î fŭnd nuŦiñ
wuz t b xpektd o Ŧt kînd, f ol Ŧ insîd o Ŧ §ip wuz
cōkt up w sand.  Hŭevr, az î had lrnd n t despᴚ o
enyŦiñ, î ryzolvd t pøl evryŦiñ t pysez Ŧt î kød o Ŧ
§ip, knklødiñ Ŧt evryŦiñ î kød g x r wød b o sum
yøz ᴙ uŦr t my.

_Mā_ 3.—î bygan w m so, & kut a pys o a bym Ŧrø, Ψic î
Ŧot held sum o Ŧ upr pʀt ᴙ quarter-deck tøgeŦr, & Ψen î

_Mā_ 4.—î went a-fishing, bt kot n 1 fi§ Ŧt î durst yt o,
til î wuz wyry o m spᴙt; Ψen, j gōiñ t lyv of, î kot a

ol Ψic î drîd in Ŧ sun, & āt Ŧem dry.

_Mā_ 5.—Wrkt on Ŧ rek; kut anuŦr bym asundr, & brot 3

_Mā_ 6.—Wrkt on Ŧ rek; got sevrl îrn bōlts ŭt o r & uŦr
pysez o ironwork.  Wrkt v hʀd, & kām hōm v muc tîrd, &

_Mā_ 7.—Went t Ŧ rek agān, n w an intent t wrk, bt fŭnd
Ŧ wāt o Ŧ rek had brōk itself dŭn, Ŧ bymz byiñ kut; Ŧt

_Mā_ 8.—Went t Ŧ rek, & kᴚyd an îrn krō t renc up Ŧ
dek, Ψic lā nŭ qît klyr o Ŧ wotr ᴙ sand.  î renct ōpen

îrn krō in Ŧ rek f nxt dā.

_Mā_ 9.—Went t Ŧ rek, & w Ŧ krō mād wā intø Ŧ body o
Ŧ rek, & felt sevrl kasx, & løsnd Ŧem w Ŧ krō, bt
kød n brāk Ŧem up.  î felt olsō a rol o Iñgli§ lyd, & kød

_Mā_ 10–14.—Went evry dā t Ŧ rek; & got a grāt meny pysez o

_Jølî_ 2.—î rynød Ŧ medisin ol Ŧ 3 wāz; & dōzd mîself

CAPTR VII—AGRIKULCRL XPYRYENS


î had nŭ byn in Ŧis unhapy îlnd abuv ten munŦs.  Ol posibility
o dylivrans x Ŧis kndi§n symd t b entîrly tākn x my;

Ψic î kød n fînd ŭt.  î srct f Ŧ cassava røt, Ψic Ŧ

î had bt nøly fini§t m fens, & bygan t enj¤ m labour, Ψen Ŧ

CAPTR VIII—SRVāZ HIZ PōZI§N


î men§nd byfᴙ Ŧt î had a grāt mînd t sy Ŧ hōl îlnd, &

wød, Ŧt î kød n sy Ψic wuz m wā bî eny dîrek§n bt Ŧt o
Ŧ sun, nᴙ yven Ŧen, unles î nø v wel Ŧ pōzi§n o Ŧ sun
at Ŧt tîm o Ŧ dā.  It hapend, t m frŦr misforcøn, Ŧt Ŧ
weŦr prøvd hāzy f 3 ᴙ 4 dāz Ψîl î wuz in Ŧ valy, &
n byiñ ābl t sy Ŧ sun, î wondrd ŭ v unkumfᴙtᴥbl, &
at last wuz oblîjd t fînd Ŧ sysîd, løk f m pōst, & kum bak

weŦr byiñ xsydiñ hot, & m gun, amøni§n, hacet, & uŦr
Ŧiñs v hevy.

In Ŧis jrny m dog srprîzd a yuñ kid, & syzd upon it; & î,
runiñ in t tāk hōld o it, kot it, & sāvd it alîv x Ŧ
dog.  î had a grāt mînd t briñ it hōm if î kød, f î had often
byn møziñ ΨeŦr it mît n b posibl t g a kid ᴙ 2, & sō

§ot §ød b ol spent.  î mād a kolr f Ŧis litl krycr, &
w a striñ, Ψic î mād o sum rope-yam, Ψic î alwāz kᴚyd
ŭ my, î led him aloñ, Ŧō w sum difikulty, til î kām t m

î kanot xpres Ψut a satisfak§n it wuz t my t kum intø m ōld

î reposed mîself hyr a wyk, t rest & rᴥgāl mîself aftr m loñ

Ŧ rāny syzon o Ŧ autumnal yqinox wuz nŭ kum, & î kept Ŧ
30th o Septembr in Ŧ sām solem manr az byfᴙ, byiñ Ŧ

It wuz nŭ Ŧt î bygan sensibly t fyl hŭ muc mᴙ hapy Ŧis lîf î

Byfᴙ, az î wokt ŭ, yŦr on m huntiñ ᴙ f vyøiñ Ŧ

T Ŧis §ᴙt tîm alŭd f labour î dyzîr mā b add Ŧ xsydiñ

Ŧis tuct my sensibly, f î fᴙso Ŧt in a fyø dāz Ŧā wød

î wuz sadly pøt t it f a sîŦ ᴙ sikl t kut it dŭn, & ol î

Hŭevr, Ŧis wuz a grāt enkrᴥjmnt t my, & î fᴙso Ŧt, in

Ŧyz Ŧiñs byiñ add t m dyzîr o haviñ a gød qontity f

It mît b trøly sed, Ŧt nŭ î wrkt f m bred.  î bylyv fyø

î, Ŧt wuz rydøst t a myr stāt o nācr, fŭnd Ŧis t m dāly

Frst, î had nō plough t trn up Ŧ rŦ—nō spād ᴙ §uvl t dig it.
Wel, Ŧis î koñkrd bî mākiñ my a wødn spād, az î obzrvd byfᴙ;

Hŭevr, Ŧis î bᴙ w, & wuz kntent t wrk it ŭt w pā§ns,

nesesᴚy f mākiñ Ŧ kᴙn, Ψen î had it, fit f m yøz.




CAPTR IX—A BōT


Bt frst î wuz t prypᴚ mᴙ land, f î had nŭ syd ynuf t sō
abuv an ākr o grŭnd.  Byfᴙ î did Ŧis, î had a wyk’s wrk at lyst
t ā my a spād, Ψic, Ψen it wuz dun, wuz bt a sᴙy 1 indyd,
& v hevy, & ryqîrd dubl labour t wrk w it.  Hŭevr, î
got Ŧrø Ŧt, & sōd m syd in 2 lʀj flat pysez o grŭnd,
az nyr m hŭs az î kød fînd Ŧem t m mînd, & fenst Ŧem in w
a gød hej, Ŧ stāx o Ψic wr ol kut of Ŧt wød Ψic î had
set byfᴙ, & nø it wød grō; sō Ŧt, in a yr’s tîm, î nø î
§ød h a qik ᴙ liviñ hej, Ŧt wød wont bt litl repair.

CAPTR X—TAMES GōTS

CAPTR XI—FîNDZ PRINT O MAN’S FøT ON Ŧ SAND

Ŧus in 2 yrs’ tîm î had a Ŧik grōv; & in 5 ᴙ six yrs’

CAPTR XII—A KāV RYTRYT


Ψîl Ŧis wuz døiñ, î wuz n oltøgeŦr kᴚles o m uŦr afᴚz;

CAPTR XIV—A DRYM RYᴥLîZD


Haviñ nŭ brot ol m Ŧiñs on §ᴙ & sekyørd Ŧem, î went bak

CAPTR XV—FRîDā’S EDøKā§N


Aftr î had byn 2 ᴙ 3 dāz rytrnd t m kasl, î Ŧot Ŧt,
in ᴙdr t briñ Frîdā of x hiz hᴙid wā o feeding, & x Ŧ

î tøk him ŭt w my 1 mᴙniñ t Ŧ wødz.  î went, indyd,

CAPTR XVII—VIZIT O MUTINEERS


In a litl tîm, hŭevr, nō mᴙ canøz apyriñ, Ŧ fyr o Ŧᴚ
kumiñ wᴙ of; & î bygan t tāk m fᴙmr Ŧots o a v¤āj t
Ŧ mān intø knsidrā§n; byiñ lîkwîz a§ørd bî Frîdā’s foŦr
Ŧt î mît dypend upon gød yøsᴥj x Ŧᴚ nā§n, on hiz akŭnt, if
î wød gō.  Bt m Ŧots wr a litl sspendd Ψen î had a syryus
diskᴙs w Ŧ Spaniard, & Ψen î undrstød Ŧt Ŧᴚ wr

Ŧ savājz, bt wr v sᴙ pøt t it f necessaries, &, indyd,
f lîf.  î askd him ol Ŧ pʀtikølrz o Ŧᴚ v¤āj, & fŭnd
Ŧā wr a Spani§ §ip, bŭnd x Ŧ Rio de la Plata t Ŧ Havanna,
byiñ dîrektd t lyv Ŧᴚ lōdiñ Ŧᴚ, Ψic wuz cyfly hîdz &
silvr, & t briñ bak Ψut Yrōpyᴥn gødz Ŧā kød myt w Ŧᴚ;
Ŧt Ŧā had 5 Pᴙcøgyz symen on bᴙd, høm Ŧā tøk ŭt o
anuŦr rek; Ŧt 5 o Ŧᴚ ōn men wr drŭnd Ψen frst Ŧ
§ip wuz lost, & Ŧt Ŧyz eskāpt Ŧrø infinit dānjrz &

xpektd t h byn dyvŭrd evry mōment.  Y tōld my Ŧā had sum
ʀmz w Ŧem, bt Ŧā wr prfektly yøslᴥs, f Ŧt Ŧā had
nyŦr pŭdr nᴙ bol, Ŧ wo§iñ o Ŧ sy haviñ sp¤ld ol Ŧᴚ

Ŧemselvz w sum fød.

î askd him Ψut y Ŧot wød bykum o Ŧem Ŧᴚ, & if Ŧā had
fᴙmd eny dyzîn o mākiñ Ŧᴚ eskāp.  Y sed Ŧā had meny
konsultā§nz ŭ it; bt Ŧt haviñ nyŦr vesl nᴙ tølz t bild

CAPTR XVIII—Ŧ §IP RYKUVRD


Ψîl wy wr Ŧus prypᴚiñ ŭr dyzînz, & had frst, bî mān

CAPTR XIX—RYTRN T EñGLND


Haviñ dun ol Ŧis î left Ŧem Ŧ nxt dā, & went on bᴙd Ŧ

tîm î sent m 2 sistrz in Ŧ kuntry a hundred pŭndz yc, Ŧā
byiñ, Ŧō n in wont, yet n in v gød srkumstansz; 1 haviñ
byn mᴚyd & left a widō; & Ŧ uŦr haviñ a huzbnd n sō kînd
t r az y §ød b.  Bt amuñ ol m rylā§nz ᴙ aqāntnsz î

my; & Ŧis grātly prplext my.

î had wuns a mînd t h gon t Ŧ Brazils & h setld mîself

Hŭevr, it wuz n rylijn Ŧt kept my x gōiñ Ŧᴚ f Ŧ

Bt, az î h sed, Ŧis wuz n Ŧ mān ñ Ŧt kept my x gōiñ

In ᴙdr t prypᴚ Ŧiñs f m gōiñ hōm, î frst (Ŧ Brazil flyt

Haviñ Ŧus setld m afᴚz, sōld m kʀgō, & trnd ol m yfekts

It z trø î had byn v unfᴙcønᴥt bî sy, & Ŧis mît b 1 o
Ŧ ryznz; bt let nō man slight Ŧ stroñ impulsz o hiz ōn

Haviñ byn Ŧus hʀast in m Ŧots, m ōld pîlᴥt, t høm î

Az î h trubld u w nun o m sy jrnlz, sō î §al trubl

Y satisfîd us Ŧt Ŧᴚ wuz nō dānjr o Ŧt kînd in Ŧ wā Ŧt wy

Wy wr a litl unyzy, hŭevr, Ψen wy fŭnd it snōd 1 hōl dā

It wuz ŭ 2 ŭrz byfᴙ nît Ψen, ŭr gîd byiñ sumŦiñ
byfᴙ us, & n j in sît, ŭt ru§t 3 monstrus wølvz, &
aftr Ŧem a bᴚ, x a holō wā aj¤niñ t a Ŧik wød; 2 o

It wuz hapy f Ŧ pør man Ŧt it wuz m man Frîdā; f, haviñ byn
yøzd t suc krycrz in hiz kuntry, y had nō fyr upon him, bt went

at a fʀŦr distns, & h prhaps yŦr mist Ŧ wølf ᴙ
endānjrd §øtiñ Ŧ man.

Bt it wuz ynuf t h tᴚifîd a boldr man Ŧan î; &, indyd, it
alʀmd ol ŭr kumpany, Ψen, w Ŧ n¤z o Frîdā’s pistl, wy
hrd on bōŦ sîdz Ŧ mōst dizml hŭliñ o wølvz; & Ŧ n¤z,
rydubld bî Ŧ ekō o Ŧ mŭntnz, apyrd t us az if Ŧᴚ had
byn a prōdijus numbr o Ŧem; & prhaps Ŧᴚ wuz n suc a fyø az
Ŧt wy had nō koz o apryhen§n: hŭevr, az Frîdā had kild Ŧis

wuz mōst hrt; f Ŧ rājiñ krycr had bit him twîs, wuns in Ŧ
ʀm, & Ŧ uŦr tîm a litl abuv hiz ny; & Ŧō y had mād
sum defence, y wuz j tumbliñ dŭn bî Ŧ disᴙdr o hiz hᴙs,
Ψen Frîdā kām up & §ot Ŧ wølf.

It z yzy t supōz Ŧt at Ŧ n¤z o Frîdā’s pistl wy ol mendd
ŭr pās, & rōd up az fast az Ŧ wā, Ψic wuz v difikult, wød
giv us lyv, t sy Ψut wuz Ŧ matr.  Az søn az wy kām klyr o
Ŧ tryz, Ψic blîndd us byfᴙ, wy so klyrly Ψut had byn Ŧ
kās, & hŭ Frîdā had disengājd Ŧ pør gîd, Ŧō wy did n
presntly disrn Ψut kînd o krycr it wuz y had kild.




CAPTR XX—FîT BYTWYN FRîDā & A Bᴚ


Bt nevr wuz a fît manājd sō hardily, & in suc a srprîziñ manr
az Ŧt Ψic folōd bytwyn Frîdā & Ŧ bᴚ, Ψic gāv us ol,
Ŧō at frst wy wr srprîzd & afrād f him, Ŧ grātst
dîver§n imajinᴥbl.  Az Ŧ bᴚ z a hevy, klumzy krycr, & duz
n galop az Ŧ wølf duz, ø z swift & lît, sō y haz 2
pʀtikølr qolityz, Ψic jenruly ʀ Ŧ røl o hiz ak§nz; frst,
az t men, ø ʀ n hiz propr prā (y duz n yø§ᴥly atemt Ŧem,
xept Ŧā frst atak him, unles y b xsesivly huñgry, Ψic it
z probbl mît nŭ b Ŧ kās, Ŧ grŭnd byiñ kuvrd w snō),
if u d n medl w him, y wil n medl w u; bt Ŧen u
must tāk kᴚ t b v sivl t him, & giv him Ŧ rōd, f y z
a v nîs jentlmn; y wil n gō a step ŭt o hiz wā f a prins;
nā, if u ʀ ryly afrād, yᴙ best wā z t løk anuŦr wā &
kyp gōiñ on; f sumtîmz if u stop, & stand stil, & løk
stedfastly at him, y tāks it f an afrunt; bt if u Ŧrō ᴙ tos
enyŦiñ at him, Ŧō it wr bt a bit o stik az big az yᴙ fiñgr,
y Ŧiñx himself abøzd, & sets ol uŦr biznes asîd t prsø hiz
ryvenj, & wil h satisfak§n in ¤ o honour—Ŧt z hiz frst
qolity: Ŧ nxt z, if y b wuns afruntd, y wil nevr lyv u,
nît ᴙ dā, til y haz hiz ryvenj, bt folōz at a gød rŭnd rāt
til y ōvrtāx u.

M man Frîdā had dylivrd ŭr gîd, & Ψen wy kām up t him y wuz
helpiñ him of hiz hᴙs, f Ŧ man wuz bōŦ hrt & frîtnd, Ψen
on a sudn wy espied Ŧ bᴚ kum ŭt o Ŧ wød; & a monstrus 1
it wuz, Ŧ bigest bî fʀ Ŧt evr î so.  Wy wr ol a litl
srprîzd Ψen wy so him; bt Ψen Frîdā so him, it wuz yzy t sy
j¤ & krᴥj in Ŧ felō’s kŭntenans.  “O! O! O!” sez Frîdā,
3 tîmz, p¤ntiñ t him; “O mastr, u giv my te lyv, my shakee
te hand w him; my makee u gød laf.”

î wuz srprîzd t sy Ŧ felō sō wel plyzd.  “U føl,” sez î,
“y wil yt u up.”—“Eatee my up! eatee my up!” sez Frîdā, twîs ovr
agān; “my eatee him up; my makee u gød laf; u ol stā hyr, my
§ō u gød laf.”  Sō dŭn y sits, & gets of hiz bøts in a
mōment, & pøts on a pᴚ o pumps (az wy kol Ŧ flat §øz Ŧā wᴚ,
& Ψic y had in hiz poket), givz m uŦr srvnt hiz hᴙs, &
w hiz gun awā y flø, swift lîk Ŧ wind.

Ŧ bᴚ wuz wokiñ softly on, & ofrd t medl w nōbudy, til
Frîdā kumiñ prity nyr, kolz t him, az if Ŧ bᴚ kød undrstand
him.  “Hʀk yā, hʀk yā,” sez Frîdā, “my speakee w u.”  Wy
folōd at a distns, f nŭ byiñ dŭn on Ŧ Gascony sîd o Ŧ
mŭntnz, wy wr entrd a vast fᴙest, Ψᴚ Ŧ kuntry wuz plān &
prity ōpen, Ŧō it had meny tryz in it skatrd hyr & Ŧᴚ.
Frîdā, ø had, az wy s, Ŧ Ψylz o Ŧ bᴚ, kām up w him
qikly, & tøk up a grāt stōn, & Ŧrø it at him, & hit him j
on Ŧ hed, bt did him nō mᴙ hʀm Ŧan if y had Ŧrōn it agānst a
wol; bt it ansrd Frîdā’s end, f Ŧ rōg wuz sō v¤d o fyr
Ŧt y did it pyørly t ā Ŧ bᴚ folō him, & §ō us sum laf
az y kold it.  Az søn az Ŧ bᴚ felt Ŧ blō, & so him, y
trnz ŭ & kumz aftr him, tākiñ v loñ strîdz, & §ufliñ
on at a strānj rāt, sō az wød h pøt a hᴙs t a midliñ galop;
awā rānz Frîdā, & tāks hiz kᴙs az if y ran tøwᴙdz us f help;
sō wy ol ryzolvd t fîr at wuns upon Ŧ bᴚ, & dylivr m man;
Ŧō î wuz añgry at him f briñiñ Ŧ bᴚ bak upon us, Ψen y wuz
gōiñ ŭ hiz ōn biznes anuŦr wā; & espe§ly î wuz añgry Ŧt
y had trnd Ŧ bᴚ upon us, & Ŧen ran awā; & î kold ŭt, “U
dog! z Ŧis yᴙ mākiñ us laf?  Kum awā, & tāk yᴙ hᴙs, Ŧt
wy mā §øt Ŧ krycr.”  Y hrd my, & krîd ŭt, “Nō §øt, nō
§øt; stand stil, & u g muc laf:” & az Ŧ nimbl krycr
ran 2 fyt f Ŧ bᴚ’s 1, y trnd on a sudn on 1 sîd o us,
& syiñ a grāt oak-tree fit f hiz prpᴥs, y bekond t us t
folō; & dubliñ hiz pās, y got nimbly up Ŧ try, lāyiñ hiz gun
dŭn upon Ŧ grŭnd, at ŭ 5 ᴙ six yʀdz x Ŧ botm o Ŧ
try.  Ŧ bᴚ søn kām t Ŧ try, & wy folōd at a distns: Ŧ
frst ñ y did y stopt at Ŧ gun, smelt at it, bt let it lî,
& up y skramblz intø Ŧ try, climbing lîk a kat, Ŧō sō
monstrus hevy.  î wuz amāzd at Ŧ foly, az î Ŧot it, o m man,
& kød n f m lîf sy enyŦiñ t laf at, til syiñ Ŧ bᴚ
g up Ŧ try, wy ol rōd nyr t him.

Ψen wy kām t Ŧ try, Ŧᴚ wuz Frîdā got ŭt t Ŧ smol end o a

î h nuŦiñ unkomn t tāk nōtis o in m pasāj Ŧrø

î wuz nŭ kum t Ŧ centre o m travlz, & had in a litl tîm ol

M prinsipl gîd & privy-counsellor wuz m gød ān§ent widō, ø,

& nŭ, haviñ ryzolvd t dispōz o m plantā§n in Ŧ Brazils, î

In rytrn, î sînd Ŧ instrumnt o sāl in Ŧ fᴙm Ψic Ŧā sent
